Hotel service: The service at Guangzhou Jinshan Hotel is highly praised. The front desk staff are friendly and professional and can provide guests with timely and effective service. The room is spacious and comfortable, with complete facilities, including an independent cloakroom and spacious bathroom space. In addition, the hotel also has an indoor swimming pool. Surrounding environment: The surrounding environment of Guangzhou Jinshan Hotel is beautiful, with beautiful views of the lake and a drying rack to dry clothes. The surrounding facilities are complete, including restaurants, conference rooms, etc., suitable for business and leisure guests.
Distance from Rexue Miracle: Rexue Miracle (Guangzhou Sunac Snow World) is one of the core businesses of Guangzhou Sunac Cultural Tourism City, not far from Guangzhou Jinshan Hotel. The hotel has a car to pick up and drop off the Snow World at any time, providing guests with convenient transportation services. Therefore, for guests who want to experience the miracle of hot snow, choosing to stay at Guangzhou Jinshan Hotel is a good choice.
In general, the service and surrounding environment of Guangzhou Jinshan Hotel are quite good. It is also relatively close to the Hot Snow Miracle and is suitable for business and leisure guests.

name:P‚Äço‚Äçw‚Äçi‚Äçc
info:Superior Lake-view Queen Room

rating:4.7
posted:Posted August 14, 2023
msg:Staying at Jinshan Hotel this time, it is only a 10-minute walk away from Sunac Mall, which is very convenient! There is a construction project opposite the front lobby of Jinshan Hotel, so it is quite dangerous for vehicles to come and go. It is recommended to go to the shopping mall by walking on the pedestrian road by the lake, passing the Grand Theater and the outdoor parking lot, and crossing a road to the shopping mall. Or you can take the hotel shuttle bus to the mall, there are two buses an hour. There is a buggy transfer at the entrance of the hotel to go to Shiberger and Shiberger Grand View Hotel, just with the concierge.

The hotel lobby has a high floor and a great sense of space. We checked in at 12:30 and already had a room. This time I chose a superior lake view room. The room is on the sixth floor non-smoking floor. The room is fully air-conditioned and decorated in a modern style. It includes 4 bottled mineral water, tea and coffee bags, toiletries, slippers, etc. The terrace view is beautiful, you can see the lake and the rest of the two hotels. The room has a large bathtub with a shower, and a large bed! Open the curtains, lean on the sofa in the room and watch the scenery, very comfortable. We asked for slippers for the kids and they were delivered to the room promptly.

The hotel has a rich selection of breakfast, different kinds of porridge and noodles, steamed dishes, sushi, Western-style buns, Western-style hot food, fruit, cheese, five-shell miscellaneous beans and ready-to-ground drinks... everything is available, suitable for the whole family. We had breakfast at 8 and there wasn't much traffic, but by the time we left at 9 it was packed. Breakfast is served from 7-10 o'clock, it is recommended to go earlier. There is a swimming pool on the 5th floor of the hotel, towels are provided, and there are coaches nearby to teach swimming, which is very good! There is also a 24-hour gym room next to it.

It is worth mentioning that the road next to the hotel is under construction, so it is not recommended to stay in a city view room, because it is really dusty and noisy. The lake view room not only has a beautiful view, but you can't even hear the sound of the construction, and the sound insulation is very good!

There are many choices of restaurants in the shopping mall, such as large chain brands such as Taier Pickled Fish, Coconut Chicken Pot, Tanyu, Laoluo Jiangxi Rice Noodles, HEYTEA, Nayuki Tea, Burger King, McDonald‚Äôs, Pizza hut‚ãØ There is a water park and For the entertainment snow area/skiing area, I bought a set ticket on the trip in advance, and there is a ticket collection office at the door to scan the QR code to pick up the ticket, which is very convenient! There are so many games to play in the sports world, buy a whole day package and play slowly! There is also a large supermarket in the ba*****t!

After we checked out at 12 o'clock, we called a taxi from the concierge to go to Guangzhou North Railway Station. It took about 15 minutes and the fare was ¬•46. We take the high-speed train from Guangzhou North to Shenzhen North, and then take the high-speed train from Shenzhen North to Hong Kong West Kowloon. It takes about one and a half minutes to return to Hong Kong, which is very convenient!
